***knaller.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:knaller.html>knaller</a> (20070)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knallen.html>knallen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knaller.html>knaller</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knallers.html>knallers</a></b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:diminutive.html>diminutive</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knaller.html>knallertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:knapp.html>knapp</a> (39335)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:low.html>Low</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml"><a href = vnd.unilang:knap.html>knap</a></i>. Cognate <a href = vnd.unilang:with.html>with</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language"><a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knap.html>knap</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:whose.html>whose</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sense.html>sense</a> “pretty” <a href = vnd.unilang:also.html>also</a> occurs <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a> attestations <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:thought.html>thought</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:be.html>be</a> derived <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> “tight” <a href = vnd.unilang:via.html>via</a> “tightly fitting” (<a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:piece.html>piece</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:clothing.html>clothing</a>). <a href = vnd.unilang:further.html>Further</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:origin.html>origin</a> unsettled.  <a href = vnd.unilang:also.html>Also</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:compare.html>compare</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">næppe</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:hardly.html>hardly</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:at.html>at</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:all.html>all</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:knippen.html>knippen</a> (5101)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:knippen.html>knippen</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:further.html>further</a> etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:unknown.html>unknown</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:directly.html>Directly</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:related.html>related</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:only.html>only</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:with.html>with</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:low.html>Low</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml"><a href = vnd.unilang:knippen.html>knippen</a></i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:probably.html>Probably</a> onomatopoeic.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>The</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sense.html>sense</a> “to blink” <a href = vnd.unilang:may.html>may</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:at.html>at</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:least.html>least</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:part.html>part</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:be.html>be</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:due.html>due</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> conflation <a href = vnd.unilang:with.html>with</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knijpen.html>knijpen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:squeeze.html>squeeze</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <a href = vnd.unilang:compare.html>Compare</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a></i> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ogen.html>ogen</a></i> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">toeknijpen</i> (“to <a href = vnd.unilang:screw.html>screw</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:up.html>up</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:one.html>one</a>’<a href = vnd.unilang:s.html>s</a> eyes”); <a href = vnd.unilang:also.html>also</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German"><a href = vnd.unilang:low.html>Low</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds"><a href = vnd.unilang:knippen.html>knippen</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">kniepen</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:both.html>both</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sense.html>sense</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> “to blink”, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language"><a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">kniepen</i>.
